深度解读携程技术出海实战。

并提供可复用的解决方案。

<!-- 图源: ./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p001_scan.jpg -->

---

## Page 2

内容简介
这是一本来自费程技术团队的解读全球业务
系统架构的实战手酬，本书系统拆解了“业务出
海”全级路面脂的技术挑战。显盖从多Region黑
狗，数据合规到用填支付等的所有核心环节，指在
都助出海全业规题各种技术始明。全书以“全球化
业务蒸地”为主线，深入部析了从策构设计、流量
调度、数据合规、基础设施，别体验优化、支付建
设、客服系统及T运维的完整技术实践，不仅覆盖
核心技术额域。更结合费程在在线脂游（OTA）顿
域的真实场景，提练出一套可复用、高可用的全球
化技术体系，适合计划或正在推进业务出海的技术
团队、架构师及决策者阅读。
全书其分为10章，逻辑上可以分为4个部分：
第1~2章：从在线图游全球化部著的挑战切
入。闻适全球化取师果狗设计思路，相助读者建
立系统果病居面的认加基础，并通过一个服务实
例，详细展示软件聚构设计思路在不同场量下的
具体应用。
第3-6章：这部分是本书的重点，对全球化的
关键系统组件进行解读，包据流量调度、数据存
储、基础设施、终端用户体验4个维度，通盖全球
不同地区的流量调度、多区城数据存储、湿合云成
本与延时优化，多云多集群标准化部署、本地化体
检以及终调性能优化等数十个典型问题。
第7~9章：聚集全球化的业务落地，系统介绍
疯程在全球视野下的金融支付系统，客户服务系
统、IT基础运维方面的实践，覆盖本地化支付渠道
接入、资金安全与质量保障体系、多语言系境、多
Region的智能客服与调度系统、海外办公环填建
设、IT系统架构与运营管理等多个典型问题，
第10章：分享费程在酒店、机票、放游、文
车票、商监等业务线全球化中的宝责经检，如全球
俱应商系境的航战及应对，酒店查询引掌本地化的
脱战及解决方案、通过机票系统策构升级解决全球
化中的数据物议碎片化及复余定价逻组问超等。

<!-- 图源: ./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p002_scan.jpg -->

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef">推 荐 序 </span><span style="font-family:'RoughSpring-Regular';font-size:14.00pt;color:#42c8f4">Foreword</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">多年来，在全球互联网产业浪潮中，我们始终以谦逊之心仰望前沿，其中硅谷的创新基</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">因、工程师文化中的极致精神，以及那些历经市场验证的技术方法论，都曾是我们反复研习</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的范本。我们的学习从来都不是简单的模仿，而是带着敬畏的“追问本质”：他们如何在规模</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化中保持系统韧性？如何让技术架构适配全球化场景的复杂变量？正是这样的思辨，支撑着</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">我们在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 余载的技术深耕中，从追随者逐步成长为行业探索者。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">如今回望，全球互联网的竞合格局一直在悄然演进中。在诸多领域，中美企业的技术路</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">径与商业实践正形成有趣的对照与互补，而全球化能力的构建，始终是绕不开的命题。我们</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">常思考：为何有些企业似乎天然具备全球化的“基因编码”，而另一些则需要在本地化与全球</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化之间艰难地寻找平衡？除了语言、文化等显性差异，技术架构的扩展性、跨区域协同的效</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">率、数据合规的边界……这些深层挑战都值得行业共同拆解。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程的国际化探索，恰是在这样的思考中逐步铺展的。从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2014</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年启动早期探索时的“摸</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">着石头过河”，到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 2017 </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">年以</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Trip.com</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 品牌为起点全面推进全球化战略，我们走过不少弯路：</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">既有过系统适配多区域法规时的技术阵痛，也经历过在跨文化场景下对用户体验进行反复调</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">校。这让我们深刻意识到，全球化从来不是简单的“复制粘贴”——要将国内已有的庞大交</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">易体系、覆盖全品类的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“一站式预订”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">能力延伸至全球市场，如何在不颠覆既有架构的前提下</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现平滑扩展？如何让供应链的全球化特性与本地化服务需求高效耦合？这些问题，倒逼我</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">们在技术层面重构底层逻辑。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2019 </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">年，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">James </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">提出的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">G2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Globalization and Great Quality</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，全球化与高品质）战略为我</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">们指明了技术演进的锚点：全球化不是单点突破，而是让“高标准用户体验”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">成为所有业务</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">线的技术基线。为此，我们启动了系统性的技术升级：从构建跨区域统一的云原生基础设施，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到开发支持多语言、多币种、多法规的本地化工具链；从搭建全球实时的用户体验监控网络，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到建立符合</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> GDPR</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">CCPA </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">等标准的数据安全治理框架……每一步都伴随着对既有系统的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“微</span>

---

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">创式改造”——既要避免“另起炉灶”，又要为全球化场景注入新的技术能力。这个过程里，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">团队常常在“兼容性”与“创新性”的张力中寻找最优解，而那些被验证有效的方法论，正</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">是本书要呈现的核心内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作为亲历者，我有幸从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2016</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年担任集团技术委员会主席起，深度参与了这一系列技术变</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">革；</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2023 </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">年接手技术中心后，我更直观地感受到全球化征程中技术决策的重量。这些年，我</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">们踩过的坑、填过的缝、在凌晨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 点的会议室里争论出的方案，最终都沉淀为技术体系里的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“抗风险基因”。正因深知每一步突破都凝结着团队的集体智慧，而非个人的灵光一闪，才更</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">不敢轻言“经验”二字——本书所呈现的，不过是我们在特定阶段、特定场景下的思考路径：</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">当既有系统遭遇全球化瓶颈时，如何平衡重构成本与业务连续性？面对多区域合规要求，技</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">术架构该如何设计“弹性边界”？这些探索或许不具备普适性，但希望能为同样走在国际化</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">道路上的同行提供一些镜鉴。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">技术的价值，永远在于解决真实世界的问题。当中国企业越来越深地参与到全球产业协</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作中，我们既需要继承那些被验证的底层逻辑，又需要在本土实践中生长出属于自己的技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">哲学。这本书若能成为一块引玉之砖，引发更多关于“全球化技术能力构建”的讨论，便已</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现了它的初衷。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">马 超  </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程技术</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">VP</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、技术委员会主席</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">  </span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">V</span>

## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef">前  言 </span><span style="font-family:'RoughSpring-Regular';font-size:14.00pt;color:#42c8f4">Preface</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">为什么要写这本书</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">近年来，中国企业加速国际化进程，积极参与全球竞争，掀起强劲的出海浪潮。众多学</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">者、企业和组织对企业出海进行了深入研究，内容涉及出海战略、法律与政策、国际市场、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">跨境电商与贸易、品牌国际化等多个领域。市场上也随之涌现出大量与出海相关的书籍，形</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">式多样，包括科研分析、行业调研、企业自传和知识分享等多种类型。然而，大多数书籍侧</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">重于业务层面的出海实践，针对技术出海的分析著作却较为少见。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作为国内知名的在线旅游平台企业，携程集团在深耕国内市场的同时，积极布局全球化</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">战略。从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2016</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年开始，携程集团启动全球化战略，目前已取得显著成绩。携程集团始终将技</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">术和服务视为核心竞争力，重视技术投入，技术实力也成为推动携程集团全球化成功的关键</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">引擎。在全球化进程中，携程技术团队在挑战中学习，在磨砺中成长，积累了许多极具价值</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的实战经验。携程集团希望将这些经验分享给有出海需求的企业，帮助它们少走弯路，因此</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">萌生了撰写本书的想法。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">借助此次写书的契机，携程技术团队对全球化实践知识进行了深度复盘和系统化梳理。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书的出版不仅为团队提供了分享经验的机会，也成为团队成员提升自身能力的重要契机。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">读者对象</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书基于技术实践撰写，因此，所有有出海业务或者需求的企业的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">CTO</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、技术负责人、技</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">术研发人员，以及对出海技术体系与方法论感兴趣的读者，都可以通过本书获得想要的知识。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">本书特色</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书以携程集团的全球化进程为背景，重点探讨携程在出海过程中面临的核心技术挑战，</span>

---

## Page 9

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">并深度剖析对应的解决策略、经验及实际案例。内容涵盖全球化软件架构、流量调度、数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">存储、基础设施、终端用户体验、客服系统、海外支付、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 基础运维以及业务出海实践等多</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">个方面。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">书中的大部分内容源于携程技术团队近年来在出海过程中积累的独到经验，这些经验可</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">能并非普适，且与携程的企业愿景、业务场景及发展历程等自身因素密切相关。因此，建议</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">读者在借鉴或参考本书内容时，务必结合自身企业的实际情况，因地制宜地制定具体的行动</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">方案。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">如何阅读本书</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书在逻辑上可分为三部分。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings-Regular';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">❑</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章和第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本部分从在线旅游（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）全球化部署面临的挑战切入，阐述全球</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化软件架构设计思路，助力读者构建系统架构层面的认知基础，并通过具体服务实例，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">详细展示软件架构设计思路在不同场景下的具体应用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings-Regular';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">❑</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> ～</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这部分是本书的重点，从全球流量调度系统、数据存储、基础设施、终</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">端用户体验等维度展开系统性阐述。其中，第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章重点介绍全球流量调度系统中关键</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">组件的设计方法，以及实现在全球不同地区进行流量调度的方法；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章介绍数据库、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">缓存、分布式存储和配置中心在全球化架构下的技术实现细节；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章介绍混合云网</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">络架构、减少延时及提升性能的方法、高效完成服务部署和可观测的方法，以及高效</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">适配多云、多集群、多语言等复杂环境的方法等重点内容，旨在构建标准化且可复制</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的全球部署能力；第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章聚焦全球化中的本地化与性能挑战，着重介绍本地化产品设</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">计、多语言质量保证及终端性能优化经验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'Wingdings-Regular';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">❑</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">7</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> ～</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">10</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这部分系统介绍携程支付系统、客户服务系统、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 基础运维及携程在</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球化方面的实践探索，并分享酒店、机票、旅游、火车票、商旅等业务线在全球化</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">中的宝贵经验，如全球供应商系统面临的挑战及其应对方法、酒店查询引擎本地化的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">解决方案、在全球化中通过架构升级来解决数据协议碎片化及机票复杂定价逻辑的方</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">法等。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZDBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">致谢</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">感谢携程技术委员会、各业务线</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">CTO</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的鼎力支持！</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">352</span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">The world is a book, and those who do not travel read only one page.</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">St. Augustine</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“世界是一本书，不旅行的人只读了一页。”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">圣奥古斯丁</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">当今时代，全球化浪潮汹涌澎湃，深刻地改变着世界的经济、文化。中国自加入世界</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">贸易组织以来，积极融入全球经济体系，在国际舞台上的地位日益提升。企业作为经济发</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">展的主体，其全球化与出海实践成为推动经济发展的重要力量。携程作为中国互联网旅游</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">行业的领军企业，在全球化的征程中积极探索，不断创新。它的出海战略不仅关乎自身的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">发展，也为中国企业在国际市场上的拓展提供了宝贵的经验和借鉴。让我们一同深入了解</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球化趋势，探寻携程的出海之路。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#00aeef">1.1</span><span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 全球化趋势</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2001</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 日，中国在卡塔尔多哈签署了加入世界贸易组织（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">WTO</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）的议定书，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">并于同年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">12</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 日正式成为第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">143</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 个成员。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">加入世界贸易组织以来，在法律法规、关税政策、开放程度和贸易便利性等方面，中</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">国不仅履行了入世承诺，而且走得更远。中国抓住了国际分工体系调整和重构的战略机遇，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">积极参与和嵌入全球价值链，目前已跃居世界第二大经济体，在电子商务等新型贸易领域</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">成为全球的引领者。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">中国自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2013</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">9</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 月在上海建立第一个自由贸易试验区以来，已分批次建成</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">21</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 个自由</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">贸易试验区和海南自由贸易港。中国已成为国际直接投资的最大目的地国家之一，在“一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">带一路”倡议和“走出去”战略的双轮驱动下，中国制造、中国资本和中国服务的国际竞</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'RoughSpring-Regular';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef">Chapter 1</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:18.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化的缘起</span>

## Page 15

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">争力取得长足发展。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.1.1 全球市场的形成</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球市场的形成本质上是人类文明突破地理壁垒、构建全球性价值交换体系的千年进</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">程。古代欧亚大陆通过丝绸之路实现有限度的文明对话，但真正意义上的全球市场“胚胎”</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">形成于大航海时代的地理连通。远洋帆船撕开了大陆间的物理屏障，香料与白银的流动催</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">生了最初的跨国贸易网络。大航海时代后，现代工业的发展、技术的革新及大规模物流体</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">系的建立，推动了世界贸易新格局的形成。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">随着全球一体化深化及数字化发展，当代全球市场呈现出多维分裂与融合并存的复杂</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">生态，如一体化与区域化重构、数字全球化与价值链重塑。传统的中心</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">–</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 边缘世界体系遭</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">遇多极化冲击，新兴经济体的技术跃迁与产业升级正改写全球分工版图。数字化浪潮也催</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">生出虚拟与实体并行的双重市场空间</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">数据流重塑贸易形态，算法定价机制挑战传统价</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">值规律，而数字货币的兴起预示着金融基础设施的范式革新。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球市场的未来形态将取决于三大核心变量的相互作用：技术创新能否突破资源环境</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">约束、制度设计能否平衡效率与公平，文明对话能否化解认知鸿沟。当物理空间的整合接</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">近地理极限，深度全球化正步入规则协同、标准兼容与价值共识的深层整合困境。这要求</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球共同体在捍卫多样性的前提下，构建包容性更强的协作框架</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">不仅是商品与资本的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">流动自由，更是知识共享的机制创新、风险共担的治理智慧、文明互鉴的伦理共识。全球</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">市场的终极命题，或许是如何将竞争性的增长逻辑升华为可持续的共生文明。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.1.2 中国企业全球化的挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">根据《财富》杂志世界</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">500</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 强企业榜单数据，中国企业从</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1995</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年的仅</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 家上榜，到</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2023</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年跨越式增长至</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">142</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 家，美国为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">139</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 家，日本为</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">40</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 家。不过值得注意的是，日美企</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">业大部分已走完全球化发展阶段，大部分已经是完全的“全球化”企业，而中国企业的全</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">球化进程仍处于战略攻坚期，面临多重维度的出海挑战。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">企业能力升级。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">正如托马斯</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">·</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">弗里德曼在《世界是平的</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">21</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 世纪简史》中所描述</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的，中国企业大多处于制造业末端，虽然具备很强的生产制造能力，但在品牌、服</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">务、科技及创新方面仍存在差距与不足，因此需要加快能力升级和技术创新，从</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">成本优势转向技术主导，企业需在科技创新、数字基建、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ESG</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Environmental</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Social</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Governance</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，环境、社会、公司）治理、标准制定等维度同步升级。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">制度摩擦。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">不同地区市场监管趋严，全球化进程将面临诸如数据主权立法、地区合</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">规政策和区域性技术标准壁垒等多重挑战。比如欧盟发布的《通用数据保护条例》（简</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">称</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GDPR</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）、《数字服务法案》（简称</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DSA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）、《欧盟无障碍法案》（简称</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">EAA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">），其中被</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">誉为“史上最严格的数据保护法”的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GDPR</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，因其适用范围广、处罚力度大，极大</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">地提升了全球企业在个人数据和隐私保护方面的合规意识与执行力度。国际政治格</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p015_img01.png)

---

## Page 16

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">局的变化同样给企业国际化数据保护体系的搭建增添了变数，国际贸易争端、双边</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">或多边条约的签署与解体、地缘政治紧张态势等，都可能直接影响海外数据中心和</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">数据传输链路的选择。企业需构建灵活且具前瞻性的全球数据合规体系，以快速响</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">应不同司法管辖区的法规要求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">文化冲突。</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这也是全球化进程中常见的挑战之一。因为不同文明基础和认知惯性，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">中西方文化和价值观存在差异，在商业实践、市场品牌、企业管理等场景中不同国</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">家的企业会有一些冲突发生。出海企业需要了解和分析目标市场的文化基因，通过</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">构建品牌故事来跨越文化鸿沟。在对齐企业战略和核心价值观的同时，需因地制宜</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">地打造产品本地化、团队本地化。这样既可消除表层的文化冲突，又可在认知维度</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现文明对话。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.1.3 携程全球化战略</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">中国经济的蓬勃发展，互联网技术的出现，极大地促进了中国在线旅游市场的发展。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程作为中国互联网旅游行业的领军企业，从一个预定平台演进到目前旅游全生态的国际</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化企业，始终致力于用高品质服务于全球用户，可谓是在线旅游市场发展的典型代表。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">1. 使命与愿景</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程的企业使命是“追求完美旅程，共建美好世界。”。携程致力于通过便捷且丰富的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">出行服务，促进跨地区的文化交流和可持续的发展</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，以建设更为美好的世界。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程的愿景是“成为世界领先、最可信赖的线上旅行品牌系列，致力为旅行者提供性</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">价比高的完美旅行”，秉持“客户为中心”的经营理念，通过紧密无缝的合作机制、一丝不</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">苟的敬业精神、真实诚信的合作理念和“多赢”的合作体系，推动旅游行业的发展</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">2. G2 战略</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程集团于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2019</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年暨集团</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">20</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 周年之际发布</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">G2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Globalization and Great Quality Strategy</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球化与高品质）战略，同时宣布“三年亚洲第一，五年全球第一”的目标。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">G2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 战略的公布，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">清晰地展现了携程推进全球化的战略目标。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Great Quality</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">（高品质）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">以客户为中心，为客户提供最佳服务是始终需坚守的原则。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程的目标是将产品和服务做到友好和便捷，提供多语言服务；要做到服务高可靠</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">和技术高可靠，从而达到全球全覆盖和最佳质量的目标。高品质始终是携程追求的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">目标，携程也一直将技术和服务视为企业的核心竞争力。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Globalization</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">（全球化）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程将兼具本土化和全球化视野，用全球智慧惠及全球客</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">户，着力构建全球化的产品、供应链、服务和品牌体系，同时，要培育和吸引全球</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化人才。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">G2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 体系下不分本土还是海外，全球携程员工将团结一致，以卓越服务品质</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">践行承诺。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2024</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年开始，携程也树立了新的市场目标：在未来</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> ～</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年，推动各业务线实现全面</span>

<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">3</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">第1 章 全球化的缘起</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p016_img01.png)

## Page 17

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">4</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">领先，使携程成为亚洲最领先的在线旅行平台。同时，坚持</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AI</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 创新、内容创新、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ESG</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（环</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">境，社会，公司）治理，助力集团成长为全球知名旅游品牌。围绕“一个核心目标，三个创</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">新点”，携程期望在努力下，可以为全球旅游业开辟广阔业绩增长空间，与生态链伙伴携手，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">成就世界上更多旅行者的完美旅行。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">3. 国际化品牌与人才建设</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程的国际化品牌建设是一场精心布局的持久战。首先，以业务出海作为打响品牌的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">先锋。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2018</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Trip.com</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 开通日语订票系统，正式进军日本市场，迈出拓展海外业务的重</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要一步。在这个过程中，携程面临着诸多挑战，如文化差异带来的预订习惯不同等。但携</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">程积极应对，通过快速调整产品以适配当地用户需求，这种灵活应变的策略为品牌赢得了</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用户的初步认可。通过打造符合当地用户习惯的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“一站式服务模式”，携程不仅满足了用户</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">多样化的需求，更助力其在全球范围内逐渐树立起便捷、高效的品牌形象。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">服务出海则为品牌的美誉度持续添砖加瓦。携程在海外多个地区建立呼叫中心，将先</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">进的服务理念和技术融入其中。通过本地化的服务团队建设及总部高品质服务模式的复刻，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现了从最初凭借产品优势吸引客户，到依靠卓越服务留住客户的转变，携程成功地将</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“高品质模式”复制到各个海外市场，进一步巩固了品牌在国际市场的地位。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">品牌突围是携程提升国际知名度的关键一环。在海外营销过程中，携程深度洞悉当地</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">市场规则，吸纳优秀的本地人才。通过与本地人才的紧密协作，将当地市场的诉求融入品</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">牌建设全过程，以此提升品牌的价值和知名度，让携程品牌在不同文化背景的市场中都能</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现深度渗透、深入人心。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在国际化人才建设方面，携程同样不遗余力。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2017</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年成立的国际化人才中心（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ITC</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">），</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">成为携程全球化人才战略的核心枢纽。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ITC </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">从内部人才培养和海外人才招募两方面入手，为</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">公司的国际化发展提供坚实的人才保障。在内部人才培养上，携程为员工搭建了国际化成</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">长的快速通道，帮助员工拓宽国际视野、提升业务能力。在海外人才招募方面，自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2014</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 年</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">启动海外校园招聘以来，大量具有国际视野的优秀人才加入携程，为团队注入多元活力和</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球视野。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#00aeef">1.2</span><span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 全球化技术挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">从单一地区扩展至全球市场，商业版图的扩张不仅意味着更广阔的市场覆盖，更对技</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">术能力提出严苛的要求，这已经超越了简单的规模扩张逻辑。面对合规性层面的法律约束</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">GDPR</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）、网络层面的延迟问题（例如跨洋往返时间延迟超过百毫秒），以及本地化层面</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的多元需求（包括语言适配、支付习惯契合等）等，技术团队只有精确洞察到全球化部署的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">核心本质和关键要素，才能有效应对这些挑战。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">本书分为三大部分，遵循从顶层设计到系统解析再到方案落地的逻辑。首先，本书从</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p017_img01.png)

---

## Page 18

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">宏观视角提出全球化部署的总体方案，通过逐步分解方案揭示整个架构中至关重要的系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">组件；其次，本书根据功能类别，对这些系统组件进行深入阐述；最后，本书分享在全球</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化进程中，对部分业务系统进行性能优化、质量管控和本地化适配的实践经验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.2.1 全球化的顶层设计</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在单一</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">机房遍布全球时，物理距离引起的网络延迟，以及因各地区合规要求造成的数据差异，会</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">对系统架构设计产生深远影响。具体而言，需要确定哪些访问链路是可接受的，是不会对</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用户体验造成显著影响的；如何存储数据才能在满足合规要求的同时，也满足业务访问需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要；合规区域具体指的是什么区域，是否可能发生变化。这些问题都需要在架构设计初期</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">找到答案。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章将从在线旅游（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）全球化部署面临的挑战入手，提出全球化软件架构设计的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">思路。在整体方案中，可以清晰地看到有哪些组件起到了关键作用。同时，用户数据合规</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">归属地（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UDL</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）的概念首次被引入。读者将在这一章中了解到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UDL</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 作为全球化部署的核心</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">概念，是根据什么信息得到具体值的，又是如何融入各个系统和组件中的，进而逐步构建</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">起完整的部署方案。在整体方案介绍完毕后，为了帮助读者更深入地理解方案，本章还准</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">备了一节内容，通过一个服务实例，从服务的角度出发，详细展示方案在不同场景下的具</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">体应用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.2.2 全球化的关键系统组件</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">根据整体方案，请求流量必须准确地进入指定</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，该</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 获得所需要的数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">后，才可以对流量进行正确处理。为了实现对来自不同地区用户的流量进行精确控制，需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要一个全局的“指挥中心”（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Universal Control Service</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UCS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）。第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章揭示了这个“指挥中</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">心”，它通过构建一套标准的全球流量调度模型，不仅能够处理各种复杂场景下的流量调度，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">还能够针对极端情况（例如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 级别的故障，数据在合规区域内的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 间进行迁移</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">等）提供一体化的解决方案。同时，本章还将探讨在流量调度中扮演关键角色的其他系统组</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">件，包括网关、微服务、消息队列和任务调度系统。这些系统组件与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UCS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 紧密协作，通过</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">解析并应用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UCS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的路由策略，实现了对实时流量和离线流量的精确调度。此外，本章还介</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">绍了各系统根据其功能的独特性，如何针对性地解决性能优化、合规性适配、数据一致性</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">保障等方面可能遇到的问题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球化数据存储绝非单一维度的技术挑战，它既要求实现数据的合规存储，又必须确</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">保各个合规区域内的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 数据的一致性；既要解决技术难题，又要权衡数据存储在公</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:4.15pt;color:#231f20">一</span><span style="font-family:'Gulim';font-size:10.50pt;color:#231f20">○</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 地域，是根据地理位置划分的隔离区域，通常是全球化架构中的基本部署单元。因为携程内部都直接用</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">，为了便于理解，所以本书后面均直接用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 表示该概念。</span>

<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">5</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">第1 章 全球化的缘起</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:3.50pt;color:#231f20">一</span><span style="font-family:'Gulim';font-size:8.50pt;color:#231f20">○</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">部署的场景中，技术人员更加关注系统的稳定性和可扩展性。然而，当</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p018_img01.png)

---

## Page 19

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">6</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">有云上的成本；除了常规数据存储，还需对配置的全球化存储进行架构升级。第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章将介</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">绍数据库、缓存、分布式存储和配置中心在全球化架构下的技术细节。在数据库方面，本</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">章将阐述如何利用数据复制中心（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">DRC</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）实现合规区内多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 间的高效数据复制，并通</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">过统一配置策略（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UCS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）进行异常数据拦截。在缓存方面，将重点解决合规区内缓存数据复</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">制和部署成本降低的问题。随后，扩展讨论了在应用全球化部署过程中，分布式存储服务</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的选择和性能优化思路。本章的结尾，读者将了解到配置中心在全球化架构部署下，在配</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">置数据模型升级、配置一致性保障和读取性能提升上等方面的深入思考。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在全球化部署的进程中，完全依赖私有云是不切实际的，混合云部署成为必然的选</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">择。在不同地区、不同云服务提供商及不同运行环境之间进行高效互联互通，在必要时采</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">UCS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 策略进行合规区域的纠偏，在合规区域内的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 间实现流量负载均衡，都需要</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">依赖跨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的流量链路。必须保证这些链路的安全、稳定和可靠，同时要尽可能地减</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">少延迟和节约成本。除了访问流量链路之外，存储产品（如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Redis</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 等）也需要依</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">赖跨</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的数据传输链路。在服务部署平台方面，由于各公有云提供的能力参差不齐，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">部署平台需要能够高效地适配多云、多集群、多语言等复杂环境，这就需要构建一套标准</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">且可复制的全球部署能力。自动弹性扩缩容能够更有效地构建具有高可用性和高韧性的站</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">点，部署平台同样需要实现弹性、标准化落地。除了服务发布，多媒体内容的发布也是需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要考虑的一个方面，在复杂的网络环境中，要确保内容能够迅速触达用户，在合规的前提</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">下能够提供流畅的访问体验。在发布交付之后，还需要考虑全球化架构下的可观测能力，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">特别是在混合云异构环境中，开发和运维团队需要能够实时掌握系统的健康状况、服务的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">性能瓶颈、故障的影响范围以及用户体验的变化趋势。这就要求构建一套具备全局视角、</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 隔离能力，以及可高度自动化采集、分析与治理数据的可观测性平台。关于这些内</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">容的详细讨论，将在第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章展开。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">全球化部署不仅要关注服务本身，还要重视终端用户的体验。用户体验可细分为本地</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">化和高性能两个维度。全球化意味可针对不同语言区域的用户，需具备支持多语言的框架</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">和兼容各种日期格式的能力。同时，由于不同地区拥有独特的文化背景，提供本地化节假</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">日日历功能有助于增强用户的文化归属感。终端性能的提升可从网络性能和页面性能两个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">层面进行。在网络性能方面，通过合理的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">CDN</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 缓存策略，可以有效减少资源传输体积和降</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">低延迟。此外，从网络协议、接入点、框架策略等多个角度进行优化，可以显著提高海外</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">App</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的网络连接成功率并减少耗时。在页面性能方面，鉴于全球用户中仍有大量用户使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">低端设备，针对低端设备进行优化是十分必要的。同时，针对不同页面场景，在适当的时</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">机进行预请求，并采用不同的渲染策略进行优化，可以进一步提升用户体验。为了准确评</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">估用户的实际体验，需要一个稳定且合规的前端全链路性能数据采集系统，并通过可视化</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">手段供技术人员分析使用。在全球化背景下，为了更好地进行数据分析，应新增地区、语</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">言等评估维度。关于终端优化的更多细节，将在第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章深入探讨。</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p019_img01.png)

## Page 20

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">1.2.3 全球化的业务落地</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'SimSun';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> ～</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章详尽阐述了全球化部署架构设计与实现的技术细节，涵盖了从全球化部署</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的原理到整体方案设计，从前端优化技术的应用到后端中间件架构的升级，以及从服务自</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">身需考虑的问题到支撑服务的基础设施建设。至此，读者应已对全球化部署架构的各个层</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">面有了深入理解。然而，针对某些特定的业务场景，读者可能仍存有疑问。为了进一步加</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">深大家对全球化部署方案的理解，本书在后续的章节中安排了众多具体的业务实施案例，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">期望读者的疑惑能够通过这些案例进一步得到解答。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">7</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章将从国内支付体系入手，简要介绍第三方支付机构的职能，进而逐步探讨公司</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">支付系统在全球化背景下的能力演进路径。全球化带来的首要挑战是支付方式的多样化以</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">及用户使用习惯的差异化，这要求支付系统能够迅速适应并融合当地主流或新兴的收单方</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">式，同时开发出符合本地用户习惯的收银台解决方案。此外，作为支付系统的核心，资金</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">安全和交易安全至关重要。在多币种交易模型中，不同货币间的转换依赖汇率，因此获取</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">准确的汇率并确保货币兑换过程中的资金安全是基础要求。在实际交易中，涉及的多方主</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">体（包括旅行社、在线旅游代理</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">、航空公司、酒店及终端用户）都极为关注支付过程</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">中的信息安全。一些地区已经制定了法律法规，对用户数据特别是信用卡数据的存储提出</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">了具体要求，因此必须确保满足这些法规要求，保障用户数据的安全。最终，作为服务系</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">统，服务质量是至关重要的。在提供多样化支付方式和流程的同时，还需采取多种措施确</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">保系统的稳定性和可靠性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">携程秉承“追求完美旅程，共建美好世界”的使命，致力于为全球用户提供卓越的旅</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">行体验。而在国际化战略中，构建全球化的客户服务体系是至关重要的环节。第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">8</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章揭示</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">了公司如何通过全球客户服务体系的建设，为客户提供全方位、多场景的沟通渠道，确保</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">他们能够迅速、便捷地获取所需的支持与服务。携程的全球呼叫中心电话系统运用尖端的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">语音技术，为客户提供高效、便捷、清晰且稳定的语音沟通体验。系统针对不同的通信渠</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">道进行优化，以提升通信的稳定性和通话质量。高效的客户服务离不开智能化服务的构建，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">各种智能化服务组件，如自动语音识别（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Automatic Speech Recognition</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">ASR</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）组件、自</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">然语言理解（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Natural Language Understanding</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">NLU</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）组件、文本转语音（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Text to Speech</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">TTS</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）组件等，能够有效辅助客户、服务座席和管理人员在处理业务时迅速做出更明智的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">决策。在智能化服务无法应对的情况下，人工座席能够提供必要的支持。此时，全球化的、</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">高效的客服分配和调度系统可确保客户在此过程中能够获得最佳的用户体验。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">除了分布于世界各地的客服团队，公司还拥有业务办公室、收购的子公司等</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">40</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 多个不</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">同类型的海外办公机构。为这些办公机构提供全球范围内的安全、稳定、高效、简洁的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">系统，以及流畅、标准化的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 管理服务，是</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 团队的核心职责与目标。第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">9</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章详细阐述</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">了</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 团队如何通过基础环境建设、</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 应用系统架构设计以及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 服务的海外运营管理</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">3</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 个</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">阶段，逐步实现既定的团队目标。鉴于不同国家和地区在法律法规、文化背景以及</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">IT</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 基础</span>

<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">7</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">第1 章 全球化的缘起</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p020_img01.png)

## Page 21

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">8</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">环境上的差异，需要制定统一的标准和流程，以确保办公基础建设、网络规划和服务区运</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">维管理的一致性。为了提升全球员工间的协作效率，需要提供标准化且易于使用的办公协</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">作工具。同时，针对不同的办公模式（包括居家办公、共享办公室、自有办公室等），还需</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要制定有效的服务规范和标准操作流程，确保为海外员工提供全球一致化的智能标准服务。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">第</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">10</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 章将深入探讨一线业务场景，涵盖供应链管理、酒店、机票及商旅服务。通过实</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">际案例，我们将深入剖析这些业务在全球化进程中遭遇的技术难题，并向读者分享相应的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">解决策略和实践经验。随着业务在全球范围内拓展，尤其是从本土进入海外市场，供应商</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">系统遭遇了众多复杂挑战。构建一个全面、高效、稳定的供应商管理系统，对携程成为全</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">球领先的在线旅游平台至关重要。针对全球化场景下的多币种和多时区计算需求，我们对</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">酒店查询引擎进行了架构升级和规范化改进。与酒店业务面临的挑战相似，机票业务系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">也需要通过架构升级和规范化改进，具备处理来自不同渠道的碎片化数据和复杂的定价逻</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">辑的能力。根据业务特性，商旅系统必须能够迅速对国际合作伙伴进行技术赋能，输出卓</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">越的商旅服务。同时，它还需解决商旅业务特有的跨时区审批时效性问题，并为全球中小</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">型企业提供标准化的差旅解决方案。</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p021_img01.png)

## Page 22

<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Simplicity is the ultimate sophistication.</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Leonardo da Vinci</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“简单是最终的复杂。”</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.14pt;color:#231f20">—</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">列奥纳多</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">·</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">达</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSJW--GB1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">·</span><span style="font-family:'FZKTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">芬奇</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在全球化部署过程中，业务层面将面临一系列新的挑战。这些挑战主要源于物理距离</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">导致的网络延迟和稳定性问题，以及各地区合规要求的差异。随着这些变量的引入，携程</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">现有的软件体系必然需要进行全面调整。考虑到公司规模庞大、团队众多且软件产品繁杂，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">我们迫切需要一个构建统一且完善的全球化解决方案。本章就围绕这一主题进行讲解，旨</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在为这一复杂需求提供系统性的思路与框架。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#00aeef">2.1</span><span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 全球化对软件架构带来的挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在全球化的大背景下，软件架构也迎来不同挑战，其中来自</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 业务场景、数据合</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">规、可用性和稳定性等方面的挑战最为突出。下面将详细阐述这些方面的挑战。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">2.1.1 来自OTA 业务场景的挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">为了讲解更清晰，这里以在线旅游业务为例。为了确保用户无论身处何地都能享受高</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">质量的在线旅游服务，最直接的方案就是在每个地区部署数据中心，做到每个用户都有一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">个物理距离上相对接近的服务节点，有效规避物理距离带来的网络延迟与不稳定性，如</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。当用户就近访问服务节点时，延迟低、响应快，用户体验自然随之提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 业务场景下，用户往往处于移动状态。许多业务场景会涉及跨地区操作。例</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">如，用户</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">a</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 住在地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，计划前往地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 旅游，在</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA App</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 上提前安排了相应的行程。在</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">第</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:12.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 章</span>

<span style="font-family:'RoughSpring-Regular';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef">Chapter 2</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:18.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化的软件架构</span>

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">10</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用户</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">a</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 到达地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 后，为了让用户在该地区依然享受低延迟体验，要引导用户就近访问该</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">地区的数据中心，以最大程度规避跨地区网络延迟，如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。但是行程信息是用户</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 创建的，地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的服务如何获取用户之前的行程状态呢？这就引出了数据同步的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">问题：如何保证多个数据中心的数据一致性？在特定情况下，我们需要一套强大可靠的数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">据复制组件来做到这一点。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 用户跨地区操作示意图</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">虽然保证多个数据中心的数据一致具有一定的复杂度，但全球数据合规要求带来的挑</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">战更大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">2.1.2 来自数据合规的挑战</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">通常来说，用户数据（如账号、订单等）需仅在法规允许的地区进行存储和处理，这一</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要求显著增加了数据存储与流量控制的复杂性。为了描述这种复杂性，我们可以引入“合</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">规区”的概念。合规区的划分以各国现行法律法规为基准，同时需系统性纳入地缘政治博</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">弈格局、数据跨境合规动态演变、基础设施区位布局及技术实施成本等多维度要素，最终</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">形成兼具合规性与商业效率的治理框架。我们希望通过合规区这一概念，来清晰直观地呈</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">现全球数据部署的布局逻辑，方便我们快速定位不同地区用户数据的移动边界，如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-3</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">所示。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">数据合规面临的最大挑战在于局部隔离性与</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">OTA</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 业务的全局性之间存在天然矛盾。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">首先，对于用户数据，我们需要设计一种机制来精准标定用户的归属地，并确保其数</span>
