<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">就近处理</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">就近访问</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">就近访问</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">重定向</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">用户</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">b</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">用户</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">c</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">用户</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">c</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-4</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 用户合规访问示意图</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">旅游</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">其次，为了让系统能够精准区分不同合规区的用户，并准确定位相关用户数据的存储</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">位置，我们需要设计一套覆盖全链路的</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">统一染色方案</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，即在手机端、接入层、应用层、控</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">制层、数据层等全流程环节对数据进行标记，从而使得系统可以不断传递用户的合规区信</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">息，如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。通过这一机制，能确保在业务生命周期的任意环节，系统总能知道当</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">前数据应该存在哪，以及当前服务的用户属于哪个合规区。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">管理层</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">应</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">用</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">层</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">数</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">据</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">层</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">接</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">入</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">层</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-5</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 请求链路示意图</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">再次，我们还需要制定一套</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">可拓展性极强的调度策略</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，并构建一个</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">总控组件</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">来承担流</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">量转发的核心工作。这些工作包括但不限于：将合规区映射为具体的网关地址，实现流量</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">比例的控制，具备流量切换能力，制定请求失败应对策略。而消息系统、任务调度系统也</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">要响应总控组件的指令，协同完成用户的跨区域业务。这也意味着，这个控制组件必须具</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">备极强的可靠性和可拓展性。控制组件是众多基础组件的底层依赖，如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p024_img01.png)

<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">我该发给谁？</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">我要转走吗？</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-6</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 总控组件控制示意图</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">2.1.3 可用性和稳定性</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">最后，业务的可用性和稳定性同样是我们考虑的重点。我们必须能够应对诸如机房火</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">灾、断电等意外情况。所以，最好的解决方案是让合规区内的</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">多个数据中心互为备份</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">。当</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">一个数据中心发生故障时，我们可以借由总控组件的切换能力，通过修改路由策略，将用</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">户的流量路由到同一个合规区内就近的另一个数据中心，如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-7</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">合规区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">合规区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">合规区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#231f20">n</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">…</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">1</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 数据中心</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">地区</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">2</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> 故障</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">数据同步</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">切换至</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">访问不通</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">用户</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-7</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 合规区内故障切换示意图</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基于上述分析，我们制定了一套统一且完善的全球化解决方案。本章后续内容将详细</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">阐述该方案的核心内容，并展示其在实际业务场景中的具体应用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-BoldMT';font-size:14.00pt;font-weight:bold;color:#00aeef">2.2</span><span style="font-family:'FZXBSK--GBK1-0';font-size:14.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 全球化软件架构的设计思路</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">技术基础设施的部署架构通常包含如下两个主要层级。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">（区域）：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">是根据地理位置划分的隔离区域，通常作为全球化架构中的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基本部署单元。在一个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">内，通常包含多个可用区（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Availability Zones</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AZs</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">），</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">这些可用区通过低延迟网络实现互联。而不同的</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">之间则保持隔离状态，彼此</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">独立运行，互不影响。</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">间的通信链路质量普遍存在延迟高、稳定性差的特点。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">AZ</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Availability Zone</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">，可用区）：</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">AZ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是同一</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 内进一步细化的隔离单元。每</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p025_img01.png)



![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p025_img02.png)

## Page 26

<span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">第2 章 全球化的软件架构</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">13</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AZ</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 在电力、网络链路等物理设施上保持独立，但在同一</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">内通过高速网络</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">实现互联，以实现低延迟和高可用性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是全球化视角下的基本单元，后续介绍将基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 级别展开，略去</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">内部多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> AZ </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">架构的具体细节。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">2.2.1 用户体验与系统稳定性</span><span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.26pt;color:#00aeef">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">全球多 Region </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">虽然单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 是全球化架构的基本部署单元，但仅依赖单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">会存在明显弊端。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">可用性：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">在复杂的全球化环境下，系统会面临</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 间的网络故障，</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 级的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">数据中心故障等极端场景。单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 架构缺乏冗余备份机制，难以有效抵御这类风</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">险，无法保障系统的稳定性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">用户体验：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">面对分布于全球各地的用户，单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">无法保证所有的用户都能以较低</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的延迟接入，这会极大影响服务的质量。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">因此，全球化架构通常不会依赖单一</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 进行部署。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">此处以图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-8</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示架构为例介绍单</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">架构的典型组成。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">对图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-8</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 中涉及的概念介绍如下。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">网关（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Gateway</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">承担了来自用户侧的第一跳流量，为用户请求与数据中心内的业</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">务应用搭建起标准、安全、高效的通信链路。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">服务（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Service</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">业务应用通常由一系列功能内聚的服务组成，通过服务间的交互实</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">现业务逻辑。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">消息队列（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">MQ</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">消息队列提供了异步通信的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">能力，通过</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Producer/Consumer</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（生产者</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">/</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 消费</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">者）模型满足业务解耦需求。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">缓存（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Cache</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Redis</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 的缓存技术在业界得</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">到了广泛使用，支撑了热点数据的高效访问。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">数据库（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">DB</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">基于</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">MySQL</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 提供了稳定可靠</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的结构化数据储存与管理服务。</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">●</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">异步任务（</span><span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">Job</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">）：</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">部分业务逻辑依赖异步触发的</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">调度任务执行，此类任务通常通过批量扫描与批</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">量执行的模式对数据进行进一步的加工或处理。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">为了支撑全球化业务的顺畅开展，多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 部</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">署成为必然的选择。在简单的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">架构下，用</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">户访问就近的数据中心，可以获得更稳定、延迟更低</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的服务。在遇到</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">级故障的时候，可以将用户</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">流量切换到其他</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的数据中心，确保服务持续</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">可用。简单的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">架构如图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-9</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">网关</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">服务</span>

<span style="font-family:'ArialMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">14</span><span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'KozMinPro-Regular';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> </span><span style="font-family:'FZLTXHK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">全球化技术架构与实战：携程出海技术实践</span>

<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Region 1</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Region 2</span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">Region </span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPS-ItalicMT';font-size:8.00pt;font-style:italic;color:#231f20">n</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">2-9</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 简单的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:9.00pt;color:#00aeef"> 架构示意图</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">简单的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 架构存在一定缺陷：用户数据只能在法律法规允许的地区进行处</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">理，仅依赖“就近访问”机制无法满足不同地区的数据合规要求。因此不能采用简单的多</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> </span>
<span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 架构，需要进一步考虑数据合规带来的架构挑战。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">2.2.2 数据合规</span><span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:16.26pt;color:#00aeef">—</span><span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:11.50pt;color:#00aeef">全球多合规区</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">“合规性优先”是全球化架构需要严格遵守的原则。数据的存储与使用必须严格遵循各</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">个国家和地区的法律法规，所有的流量调度策略与应用处理逻辑都应该与底层数据的合规</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">属性相适配。为了更好地描述数据在全球化架构下的分布逻辑与流转边界，需要再引入</span><span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">合</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZHTK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">规区</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">（</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Compliance Area</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">）的概念。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZLTHK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#00aeef">1. 合规区（Compliance Area）</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">通常情况下，一个合规区包含多个</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">Region</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">，这些</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">都能满足数据合规的要求。在</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">同一个合规区内，数据可以合法、合规地进行存储和使用；不同的合规区之间，数据则处</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">于严格隔离状态，以防止非法跨区交流。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">为了满足合规要求，数据分布必须遵循“在合规区内封闭”的原则，坚决杜绝非法跨</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">合规区的流动。基于合规原则，不同</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> Region </span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">的数据中心会被划分到不同的逻辑合规区中，</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用户的数据仅能在该用户所属的合规区内被处理。图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-10</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示是合规区的概念示意。</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">用户在进行全球旅行时，发起的请求最初可能会优先连接到就近的数据中心网络接入</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">点。为了严格保证数据合规，用户流量需要在接入点网关被进一步转发到对应的合规区内</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">进行处理。为了实现这个目的，需要引入图</span><span style="font-family:'TimesNewRomanPSMT';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20">2-11</span><span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:10.00pt;color:#231f20"> 所示的组件。</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">缓存</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">缓存</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">缓存</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">数据库</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">数据库</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">数据库</span>

<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">异步任务</span>
<span style="font-family:'FZSSK--GBK1-0';font-size:8.00pt;color:#231f20">异步任务</span>

![](./9787111795346_全球化技术架构与实战 携程出海技术实践_assets/images/p027_img01.png)
